<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настигнуть.html>насти́гнуть</a> (9691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сти́гнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stígnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настигнуть.html>насти́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastígnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настигать.html>настига́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch up <i>(with)</i>, to come close <i>(to)</i>, to approach</li>
<li>to catch</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настил.html>насти́л</a> (13135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>

***настольный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настольный.html>насто́льный</a> (8989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настольный.html>насто́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastólʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tabletop, desktop</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

Зализняка — 1*a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-столь-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настраивать.html>настра́ивавший</a> (13625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to tune, to tune up, to adjust, to customize <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to modify</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<li>to incline <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prótiv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive against</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to incite, to make <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. someone sad/joyful</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***настроение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ние</a> (1329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastrojénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mood, spirits (mental state)</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>predisposed, inclined <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to do something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:настроенный.html>настро́ен</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спорить.html>спо́рить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>nastrójen</b> spóritʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not inclined to argue</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>in a (given) mood
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:настроенный.html>настро́ен</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on xorošó <b>nastrójen</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is in a good mood</span></div></dd></dl></li>
